\xd0\x91\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0, \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd, (\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4. ashkuza; \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82. \xe5\xa1\x9e \xe2\x80\x94 Sai, \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0: *s\xc9\x99k).\n

\xd0\x9e\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 (\xd0\xb3\xd1\x80. skythai) \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbb \xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\x93\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xc2\xab\xd0\xa2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xc2\xbb \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5, 5 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0, \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa1\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd \xc2\xab\xd0\x96\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xc2\xbb \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd.\n

\xd0\xa1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80.

\xd0\x91\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xa1\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd \xc2\xab\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xc2\xbb \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd2\xaf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xc2\xab\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xc2\xbb (\xc2\xab\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xc2\xbb, \xc2\xab\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xc2\xbb \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd) \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96.[2]\n

I-\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3\xd0\xb6\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xa1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd2\xae\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b, \xd0\x90\xd1\x83\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b, \xd0\x9e\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x90\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xbe\xd2\xa3\xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd2\xa3-\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xc2\xab\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xc2\xbb \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x93\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 (\xd0\xb1. \xd0\xb7. \xd0\xb1. V \xd2\x93.) \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\x90\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd.\n

F\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\x9e\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x90\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x83\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd3\x99\xd0\xb9\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81 \xd0\xa8\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88 (\xd0\xa2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b), \xd0\xa1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\x91\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b: \xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xe2\x80\x94 \xd0\x96\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0, \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd0\x90\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb \xd3\xa9\xd2\xa3\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0. \xd0\x86\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x91\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80, \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xba, \xd0\xa2\xd2\xaf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd, \xd0\x9a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd, \xd0\x90\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x9e\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd2\xaf\xd1\x88 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x82\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb4\xd3\x99\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96 \xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x96\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5 \xe2\x80\x94 \xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb, \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b-\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb; \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0-\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b; \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0-\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd0\xba \xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80. \xd0\xa1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9-\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b \xd0\xba\xd3\xa9\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd3\x99\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd3\xa9\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b. \xd0\x93\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf\xd1\x81 \xe2\x80\x94 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x9f\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 - \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b.\n

\xd0\xa1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd2\xaf\xd1\x88 \xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80: \xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96, \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf \xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd. \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x82\xd3\xa9\xd1\x80\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbe\xd2\xa3, \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb, \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd2\x9b\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd. \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x88 \xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd2\xaf\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96 \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd2\x9b\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b \xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x91\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 - \xd0\xba\xd2\xaf\xd0\xbd, \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbf\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb6\xd3\x99\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 4 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x96. \xd0\x91\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd2\x9a\xd2\xb1\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xba \xd0\xb6\xd2\xaf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n
